            FROM wp_rg_lead l
            INNER JOIN wp_rg_lead_detail d ON d.lead_id = l.id
            INNER JOIN
            (
                SELECT @rownum:=@rownum + 1 as sort, id
                FROM
                (
                    SELECT distinct l.id
                    FROM wp_rg_lead l
                    INNER JOIN wp_rg_lead_detail d ON d.lead_id = l.id
                    
                    WHERE (l.id = 549)
                    ORDER BY (l.id+0) DESC
                    LIMIT 0,1
                ) page
            ) filtered ON filtered.id = l.id

            ORDER BY filtered.sort

            SELECT filtered.sort, l.*, d.field_number, d.value
            FROM wp_rg_lead l
            INNER JOIN wp_rg_lead_detail d ON d.lead_id = l.id
            INNER JOIN
            (
                SELECT @rownum:=@rownum + 1 as sort, id
                FROM
                (
                    SELECT distinct l.id
                    FROM wp_rg_lead l
                    INNER JOIN wp_rg_lead_detail d ON d.lead_id = l.id
                    
                    WHERE (l.id = 550)
                    ORDER BY (l.id+0) DESC
                    LIMIT 0,1
                ) page
            ) filtered ON filtered.id = l.id

            ORDER BY filtered.sort

            SELECT filtered.sort, l.*, d.field_number, d.value
            FROM wp_rg_lead l
            INNER JOIN wp_rg_lead_detail d ON d.lead_id = l.id
            INNER JOIN
            (
                SELECT @rownum:=@rownum + 1 as sort, id
                FROM
                (
                    SELECT distinct l.id
                    FROM wp_rg_lead l
                    INNER JOIN wp_rg_lead_detail d ON d.lead_id = l.id
                    
                    WHERE (l.id = 553)
                    ORDER BY (l.id+0) DESC
                    LIMIT 0,1
                ) page
            ) filtered ON filtered.id = l.id

            ORDER BY filtered.sort

2015-05-25 21:12:49 - DEBUG --> 
            SELECT filtered.sort, l.*, d.field_number, d.value
            FROM wp_rg_lead l
            INNER JOIN wp_rg_lead_detail d ON d.lead_id = l.id
            INNER JOIN
            (
                SELECT @rownum:=@rownum + 1 as sort, id
                FROM
                (
                    SELECT distinct l.id
                    FROM wp_rg_lead l
                    INNER JOIN wp_rg_lead_detail d ON d.lead_id = l.id
                    
                    WHERE (l.form_id=49 AND l.status = 'active')
                    ORDER BY (l.id+0) DESC
                    LIMIT 0,20
                ) page
            ) filtered ON filtered.id = l.id

            ORDER BY filtered.sort

            SELECT filtered.sort, l.*, d.field_number, d.value
            FROM wp_rg_lead l
            INNER JOIN wp_rg_lead_detail d ON d.lead_id = l.id
            INNER JOIN
            (
                SELECT @rownum:=@rownum + 1 as sort, id
                FROM
                (
                    SELECT distinct l.id
                    FROM wp_rg_lead l
                    INNER JOIN wp_rg_lead_detail d ON d.lead_id = l.id
                    
                    WHERE (l.id = 560)
                    ORDER BY (l.id+0) DESC
                    LIMIT 0,1
                ) page
            ) filtered ON filtered.id = l.id

            ORDER BY filtered.sort

            FROM wp_rg_lead l

            (

                (

                    INNER JOIN wp_rg_lead_detail d ON d.lead_id = l.id

            ) filtered ON filtered.id = l.id

            FROM wp_rg_lead l
            INNER JOIN wp_rg_lead_detail d ON d.lead_id = l.id
            INNER JOIN
            (

                FROM
                (
                    SELECT distinct l.id

                    INNER JOIN wp_rg_lead_detail d ON d.lead_id = l.id
